PKP/OJS multi-source journal enrichment

This notebook adds the complete available OpenAlex and Crossref journal responses to ten real PKP OJS rows. It matches records by exact ISSN. The ten rows were chosen to include missing ISSNs, no matches, one match, and multiple matches. This sample checks whether the code works; it does not measure coverage across the full dataset.

Set OPENALEX_API_KEY in the environment or the repository-root .env file before rendering. This notebook runs the ten-row sample. Before a formal full-cohort run, replace the sections marked FULL-COHORT REPLACEMENT with reviewed batching, caching, checkpointing, and error-provenance code.

Packages and paths

This chunk loads the required R packages and sets the sample input and output paths. It first looks for OPENALEX_API_KEY in the current environment and then in the repository-root .env file.

The commented lines mark the path replacement required for a formal full-cohort run.

ISSN preparation

ISSNs may contain spaces, punctuation, or more than one value. This chunk converts each valid ISSN to the same XXXX-XXXX format and checks its final digit. It keeps missing, invalid, and valid-but-unmatched ISSNs as separate cases.

normalize_issn <- function(value) {
  compact <- gsub("[^0-9X]", "", toupper(trimws(as.character(value))))
  if (!grepl("^[0-9]{7}[0-9X]$", compact)) return(NA_character_)

  digits <- as.integer(strsplit(substr(compact, 1, 7), "")[[1]])
  check_value <- (11 - sum(digits * 8:2) %% 11) %% 11
  expected <- if (check_value == 10) "X" else as.character(check_value)
  if (substr(compact, 8, 8) != expected) return(NA_character_)

  paste0(substr(compact, 1, 4), "-", substr(compact, 5, 8))
}

parse_issns <- function(value) {
  if (is.na(value) || !nzchar(value)) return(character())

  tokens <- unlist(strsplit(value, "[[:space:],;|]+"))
  normalized <- vapply(tokens[nzchar(tokens)], normalize_issn, character(1))
  unique(normalized[!is.na(normalized)])
}

source_issns <- function(source) {
  values <- c(unlist(source$issn, use.names = FALSE), source$issn_l)
  normalized <- vapply(values, normalize_issn, character(1))
  unique(normalized[!is.na(normalized)])
}

Source retrieval

The sample sends all valid ISSNs to OpenAlex in one request. It asks Crossref about each ISSN separately and waits between requests. A Crossref 404 means that no journal record was found.

For a formal full-cohort run, replace this chunk. The full version must divide requests into small groups, read every page of results, identify the project to Crossref, retry temporary failures, save progress, and record which ISSNs failed.

fetch_openalex_sources <- function(
  issns,
  api_key = Sys.getenv("OPENALEX_API_KEY")
) {
  stopifnot(length(issns) <= 100L, nzchar(api_key))

  request("https://api.openalex.org/sources") |>
    req_url_query(
      filter = paste0("issn:", paste(issns, collapse = "|")),
      per_page = 100,
      api_key = api_key
    ) |>
    req_timeout(seconds = 30) |>
    req_perform() |>
    resp_body_json(simplifyVector = FALSE) |>
    pluck("results")
}

fetch_crossref_journal <- function(issn) {
  response <- request(paste0("https://api.crossref.org/journals/", issn)) |>
    req_timeout(seconds = 30) |>
    req_error(
      is_error = \(response) {
        resp_status(response) != 404L && resp_is_error(response)
      }
    ) |>
    req_perform()
  if (resp_status(response) == 404L) return(NULL)
  resp_body_json(response, simplifyVector = FALSE)$message
}

# FULL-COHORT REPLACEMENT:
# - send OpenAlex ISSNs in groups of at most 100 and read every result page;
# - identify Crossref requests with CROSSREF_MAILTO and use its request rate;
# - retry temporary failures, save responses, and record failed ISSNs.

Multi-source enrichment

For each PKP row, the sample looks for OpenAlex and Crossref records with the same ISSN. If the same source record appears more than once, it is counted once. Every returned top-level API field becomes a dataframe column; nested objects and arrays are stored as JSON in their field columns, and the complete candidate lists are also retained as lossless JSON.

Sample matching helpers

These helpers label each row as having no usable ISSN, no match, one match, or multiple matches. They also identify Crossref records by their ISSNs and convert every candidate field into a dataframe-safe value without filtering the response schema.

classify_status <- function(input_issns, candidate_ids) {
  case_when(
    length(input_issns) == 0L ~ "not_attempted",
    length(candidate_ids) == 0L ~ "unmatched",
    length(candidate_ids) == 1L ~ "consistent",
    TRUE ~ "inconsistent"
  )
}

crossref_key <- function(journal) {
  issns <- vapply(journal$ISSN, normalize_issn, character(1))
  paste(sort(unique(issns[!is.na(issns)])), collapse = "|")
}

serialize_json <- function(value) {
  as.character(jsonlite::toJSON(
    value,
    auto_unbox = TRUE,
    null = "null",
    na = "null",
    digits = NA
  ))
}

dataframe_value <- function(value) {
  if (is.null(value) || !length(value)) return(NA)
  if (is.atomic(value) && length(value) == 1L) return(value)
  serialize_json(value)
}

candidate_prefix <- function(prefix, index) {
  if (index == 1L) prefix else paste0(prefix, "_candidate_", index)
}

candidate_field_names <- function(match, prefix) {
  unlist(imap(match$candidates, \(candidate, index) {
    paste(candidate_prefix(prefix, index), names(candidate), sep = "_")
  }), use.names = FALSE)
}

expand_candidate_fields <- function(match, prefix) {
  cells <- list()
  for (index in seq_along(match$candidates)) {
    candidate <- match$candidates[[index]]
    values <- map(candidate, dataframe_value)
    names(values) <- paste(
      candidate_prefix(prefix, index),
      names(candidate),
      sep = "_"
    )
    cells <- c(cells, values)
  }
  cells[[paste0(prefix, "_candidates__json")]] <- serialize_json(
    match$candidates
  )
  as_tibble(cells, .name_repair = "check_unique")
}

Sample enrichment orchestration

This chunk collects the unique sample ISSNs, retrieves source records, matches them to the PKP rows, adds every returned source field, and writes one CSV row for each PKP row. The first candidate uses the ordinary source prefix; additional candidates use numbered prefixes so inconsistent matches remain complete and auditable.

For a formal full-cohort run, replace this chunk with the full version described in the comments at its end.

input_issns <- map(ojs_rows$issn, parse_issns)
tokens <- sort(unique(unlist(input_issns)))

openalex_sources <- fetch_openalex_sources(tokens)
crossref_journals <- set_names(
  map(tokens, \(token) {
    journal <- fetch_crossref_journal(token)
    Sys.sleep(0.25)
    journal
  }),
  tokens
)

openalex_matches <- map(input_issns, \(issns) {
  candidates <- keep(openalex_sources, \(source) {
    any(issns %in% source_issns(source))
  })
  candidate_ids <- map_chr(candidates, "id")
  candidates <- candidates[!duplicated(candidate_ids)]
  candidate_ids <- unique(candidate_ids)

  list(
    status = classify_status(issns, candidate_ids),
    matched_issns = intersect(
      issns,
      unique(unlist(map(candidates, source_issns)))
    ),
    candidate_ids = candidate_ids,
    candidates = candidates
  )
})

crossref_matches <- map(input_issns, \(issns) {
  matched_issns <- keep(issns, \(issn) {
    !is.null(crossref_journals[[issn]])
  })
  candidates <- unname(crossref_journals[matched_issns])
  candidate_ids <- map_chr(candidates, crossref_key)
  candidates <- candidates[!duplicated(candidate_ids)]
  candidate_ids <- unique(candidate_ids)

  list(
    status = classify_status(issns, candidate_ids),
    matched_issns = matched_issns,
    candidate_ids = candidate_ids,
    candidates = candidates
  )
})

openalex_data <- map_dfr(
  openalex_matches,
  expand_candidate_fields,
  prefix = "openalex"
)
crossref_data <- map_dfr(
  crossref_matches,
  expand_candidate_fields,
  prefix = "crossref"
)

result <- ojs_rows |>
  mutate(
    identifier_status = case_when(
      is.na(issn) | !nzchar(issn) ~ "missing",
      lengths(input_issns) == 0L ~ "invalid",
      TRUE ~ "valid"
    ),
    openalex_input_issns = map_chr(input_issns, paste, collapse = "|"),
    openalex_matched_issns = map_chr(
      openalex_matches,
      \(match) paste(match$matched_issns, collapse = "|")
    ),
    openalex_match_status = map_chr(openalex_matches, "status"),
    openalex_candidate_ids = map_chr(
      openalex_matches,
      \(match) paste(match$candidate_ids, collapse = "|")
    ),
    crossref_input_issns = map_chr(input_issns, paste, collapse = "|"),
    crossref_matched_issns = map_chr(
      crossref_matches,
      \(match) paste(match$matched_issns, collapse = "|")
    ),
    crossref_match_status = map_chr(crossref_matches, "status"),
    crossref_candidate_issn_sets = map_chr(
      crossref_matches,
      \(match) paste(match$candidate_ids, collapse = ";")
    )
  ) |>
  bind_cols(openalex_data, crossref_data)

write_csv(result, output_path, na = "")

# FULL-COHORT REPLACEMENT:
# - send OpenAlex requests in groups and read every result page;
# - save API responses so an interrupted run can continue;
# - retry temporary failures and record failed ISSNs;
# - record file checksums and run details in the metadata file.

Checks

These checks confirm that every input row appears in the output, every returned top-level API field is retained, the lossless candidate JSON matches the fetched records, the CSV file was written, and the sample contains the expected match outcomes.

expected_openalex_columns <- unique(unlist(map(
  openalex_matches,
  candidate_field_names,
  prefix = "openalex"
)))
expected_crossref_columns <- unique(unlist(map(
  crossref_matches,
  candidate_field_names,
  prefix = "crossref"
)))

stopifnot(
  exists("fetch_openalex_sources", mode = "function"),
  exists("fetch_crossref_journal", mode = "function"),
  nrow(result) == nrow(ojs_rows),
  file.exists(output_path),
  all(c(
    "openalex_match_status",
    "openalex_id",
    "openalex_summary_stats",
    "openalex_topics",
    "openalex_candidate_2_id",
    "openalex_candidates__json",
    "crossref_match_status",
    "crossref_title",
    "crossref_counts",
    "crossref_coverage",
    "crossref_candidates__json"
  ) %in% names(result)),
  all(expected_openalex_columns %in% names(result)),
  all(expected_crossref_columns %in% names(result)),
  identical(
    result$openalex_candidates__json,
    map_chr(openalex_matches, \(match) serialize_json(match$candidates))
  ),
  identical(
    result$crossref_candidates__json,
    map_chr(crossref_matches, \(match) serialize_json(match$candidates))
  ),
  all(c(
    "consistent",
    "unmatched",
    "inconsistent",
    "not_attempted"
  ) %in% result$openalex_match_status),
  "not_attempted" %in% result$crossref_match_status
)
